Introduction

Base URL: http://localhost:8002

This documentation aims to provide all the information you need to work with our API.

As you scroll, you'll see code examples for working with the API in different programming languages in the dark area to the right (or as part of the content on mobile). You can switch the language used with the tabs at the top right (or from the nav menu at the top left on mobile).

Authenticating requests

This API is not authenticated.

Categories

List all categories

Get a list of product categories with hierarchical support.

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost:8002/api/get-all-categories?parent_id=1&root=1&featured=1&with_children=1&with_parent=1&paginate=1&per_page=20" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8002/api/get-all-categories"
);

const params = {
    "parent_id": "1",
    "root": "1",
    "featured": "1",
    "with_children": "1",
    "with_parent": "1",
    "paginate": "1",
    "per_page": "20",
};
Object.keys(params)
    .forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());

Example response (200):

Show headers 
cache-control: no-cache, private
content-type: application/json
x-ratelimit-limit: 60
x-ratelimit-remaining: 59
access-control-allow-origin: *
 

{
    "success": true,
    "message": "Success",
    "data": []
}
Received response:
Request failed with error:


Tip: Check that you're properly connected to the network.
If you're a maintainer of ths API, verify that your API is running and you've enabled CORS.
You can check the Dev Tools console for debugging information.

Request      

GET api/get-all-categories

Headers

Content-Type      

Example: application/json

Accept      

Example: application/json

Query Parameters

parent_id   integer  optional  

Filter by parent category ID. Example: 1

root   boolean  optional  

Get only root categories (no parent). Example: true

featured   boolean  optional  

Filter by featured status. Example: true

with_children   boolean  optional  

Include children categories. Example: true

with_parent   boolean  optional  

Include parent category. Example: true

paginate   boolean  optional  

Enable or disable pagination (default: true). Set to 'false' for all items. Example: true

per_page   integer  optional  

The number of items per page. Example: 20

List all categories

Get a list of product categories with hierarchical support.

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost:8002/api/v1/categories?parent_id=1&root=1&featured=1&with_children=1&with_parent=1&paginate=1&per_page=20" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8002/api/v1/categories"
);

const params = {
    "parent_id": "1",
    "root": "1",
    "featured": "1",
    "with_children": "1",
    "with_parent": "1",
    "paginate": "1",
    "per_page": "20",
};
Object.keys(params)
    .forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());

Example response (400):

Show headers 
cache-control: no-cache, private
content-type: application/json
x-ratelimit-limit: 60
x-ratelimit-remaining: 48
access-control-allow-origin: *
 

{
    "status": "error",
    "message": "API key missing"
}
Received response:
Request failed with error:


Tip: Check that you're properly connected to the network.
If you're a maintainer of ths API, verify that your API is running and you've enabled CORS.
You can check the Dev Tools console for debugging information.

Request      

GET api/v1/categories

Headers

Content-Type      

Example: application/json

Accept      

Example: application/json

Query Parameters

parent_id   integer  optional  

Filter by parent category ID. Example: 1

root   boolean  optional  

Get only root categories (no parent). Example: true

featured   boolean  optional  

Filter by featured status. Example: true

with_children   boolean  optional  

Include children categories. Example: true

with_parent   boolean  optional  

Include parent category. Example: true

paginate   boolean  optional  

Enable or disable pagination (default: true). Set to 'false' for all items. Example: true

per_page   integer  optional  

The number of items per page. Example: 20

Endpoints

GET api/user

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost:8002/api/user" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8002/api/user"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());

Example response (401):

Show headers 
cache-control: no-cache, private
content-type: application/json
access-control-allow-origin: *
 

{
    "message": "Unauthenticated."
}

If you're a maintainer of ths API, verify that your API is running and you've enabled CORS.
You can check the Dev Tools console for debugging information.

class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"background-color: transparent; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);\">Types Of Acer Laptops</span></h2><p><br></p><p><br></p><h3><span class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"background-color: transparent; color: rgb(67, 67, 67);\">1. Acer Aspire</span></h3><p><br></p><p class=\"ql-align-justify\"><span class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); color: rgb(17, 17, 17);\">From entry-level laptops from the Acer Aspire 3 series to powerful laptops with many extras from the Acer Aspire 7 series. Everybody can find a suitable laptop in the Acer Aspire line. It makes no difference if you watch television shows, browse the internet, or use complex video editing software like Adobe Premiere Pro. You can always find an Acer Aspire that fulfills your needs.</span></p><p><br></p><p class=\"ql-align-justify\"><strong class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); color: rgb(17, 17, 17);\">Pros of the Acer Aspire:</strong></p><ol><li data-list=\"bullet\" class=\"ql-align-justify\"><span class=\"ql-ui\" contenteditable=\"false\"></span><span class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"color: rgb(17, 17, 17); background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">A lot of choices, divided over 3 series:</span></li><li data-list=\"bullet\" class=\"ql-align-justify\"><span class=\"ql-ui\" contenteditable=\"false\"></span><span class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"color: rgb(17, 17, 17); background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">Acer Aspire 3: basic</span></li><li data-list=\"bullet\" class=\"ql-align-justify\"><span class=\"ql-ui\" contenteditable=\"false\"></span><span class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"color: rgb(17, 17, 17); background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">Acer Aspire 5: mid-range</span></li><li data-list=\"bullet\" class=\"ql-align-justify\"><span class=\"ql-ui\" contenteditable=\"false\"></span><span class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"color: rgb(17, 17, 17); background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">Acer Aspire 7: high-end</span></li></ol><p><br></p><h3><br></h3><h3><span class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"background-color: transparent; color: rgb(67, 67, 67);\">2. Payment Gateways

APIs for handling payment gateway integrations.

Initiate NIC Asia Payment

Generates the signed payload for CyberSource/NIC Asia payment form.

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://localhost:8002/api/v1/payment/nicasia/initiate" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"order_id\": \"porro\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8002/api/v1/payment/nicasia/initiate"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "order_id": "porro"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());
Received response:
Request failed with error:


Tip: Check that you're properly connected to the network.
If you're a maintainer of ths API, verify that your API is running and you've enabled CORS.
You can check the Dev Tools console for debugging information.

Headers

Content-Type      

Example: application/json

Accept      

Example: application/json

Body Parameters

The id of an existing record in the orders table. Example: porro

Products

List all products

Get a list of products with optional filtering, sorting, and searching.

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost:8002/api/get-all-products?search=iphone&category_id=1&brand_id=2&min_price=100&max_price=1000&is_featured=1&sort=newest&include=brand%2Ccategories&page=1&per_page=15" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8002/api/get-all-products"
);

const params = {
    "search": "iphone",
    "category_id": "1",
    "brand_id": "2",
    "min_price": "100",
    "max_price": "1000",
    "is_featured": "1",
    "sort": "newest",
    "include": "brand,categories",
    "page": "1",
    "per_page": "15",
};
Object.keys(params)
    .forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());

Example response (200):

Show headers 
cache-control: no-cache, private
content-type: application/json
x-ratelimit-limit: 60
x-ratelimit-remaining: 57
access-control-allow-origin: *
 

{
    "success": true,
    "data": [],
    "meta": {
        "current_page": 1,
        "per_page": 15,
        "total": 0,
        "last_page": 1
    }
}
Received response:
Request failed with error:


Tip: Check that you're properly connected to the network.
If you're a maintainer of ths API, verify that your API is running and you've enabled CORS.
You can check the Dev Tools console for debugging information.

Request      

GET api/get-all-products

Headers

Content-Type      

Example: application/json

Accept      

Example: application/json

Query Parameters

search   string  optional  

Search term for product name, highlights, or description. Example: iphone

category_id   integer  optional  

Filter by category ID. Example: 1

brand_id   integer  optional  

Filter by brand ID. Example: 2

min_price   number  optional  

Filter by minimum price. Example: 100

max_price   number  optional  

Filter by maximum price. Example: 1000

is_featured   boolean  optional  

Filter by featured status. Example: true

sort   string  optional  

Sort option (price_asc, price_desc, name_asc, name_desc, newest). Example: newest

include   string  optional  

Comma-separated list of relationships to include (brand, categories, vendor, variants). Example: brand,categories

page   integer  optional  

The page number. Example: 1

per_page   integer  optional  

The number of items per page. Example: 15

List all products

Get a list of products with optional filtering, sorting, and searching.

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost:8002/api/v1/products?search=iphone&category_id=1&brand_id=2&min_price=100&max_price=1000&is_featured=1&sort=newest&include=brand%2Ccategories&page=1&per_page=15" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8002/api/v1/products"
);

const params = {
    "search": "iphone",
    "category_id": "1",
    "brand_id": "2",
    "min_price": "100",
    "max_price": "1000",
    "is_featured": "1",
    "sort": "newest",
    "include": "brand,categories",
    "page": "1",
    "per_page": "15",
};
Object.keys(params)
    .forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
